      <p> The Red Snakes syndicate are conspiring to collect protection money for an unknown purpose. </p>  <p> The syndicates usual gathering venue is <a href="/sandbox/nTR8nJOW/location/fKwadJrc"><strong>"The Lost Stone Tavern"</strong></a> in <strong>Palemoon</strong> </p> 
      <p> The syndicate leader is a <strong>Lanthar Admiranda</strong>, a level 6 Half-Elf Rogue.  He has piercing dark eyes, a long brown beard and stained clothes (<em>Nervous</em>). <small>In the pocket: <strong>a dirty handkerchief</strong> and <strong>5 sp</strong>.</small>   </p>
